#Tilsalg #SÃ¦lges #StineGoya #DesignersRemix #HÃ¥rbÃ¸jle #HÃ¥rbÃ¸jler #HÃ¥rpynt #kÃ¸benhavn #NÃ¸rrebro #Genbrugsmaterialer #Recycle #Recycled #Genbrugsguld #Danishdesign #Denmark #Danmark #Forsale #guld #Genbrug  #Diadem #Diademer #Hairband #Ganni #Danishdesign #Blogger #KÃ¸benhavn #Scandinaviandesign #BÃ¦redygtigt #BÃ¦redygtigtDesignBLAA GALLERI is pleased to announce ON THE OTHER SIDE - a solo exhibition by Christian Gundtoft 9/3 â€“ 5/4 2019

Opening on the 9th of March 2019 at 5:00 PM

Last time Christian Gundtoft had a solo exhibition here at BLAA, in 2018, it was called ON THE BRINK. This time around he finds himself on the other side, on the other side of what he was on the brink to - it can be understood as a reference to his artistic process. Constantly experimenting and evolving, always on the lookout for that one source of inspiration that never seizes up. He has as of late been working tirelessly on an amalgamation of his various styles and modes of expression in his painting, and the result is this exhibition. 
The exhibition title can also be understood as a reference to the motives in the artworks themselves. Christian purposefully wants them to be ambiguous as to what the motive really is, and offers a plethora of alternative interpretations, each one as valid, strong and believable as the other.

Rest assured, Christianâ€™s paintings are as surrealistic and expressive as ever, gritty and explosive, bristling with detail. The compositions are akin to an expanding chaos, yet upon close scrutiny recognizable shapes and familiar objects become crystalized and take over the narrative of the painting which opens for widely different interpretations.

For this exhibition we will present Christian Gundtoftâ€™s most recent works, presented to the public for the very first time. On the opening night, we will also have a musical contribution from Linebug, an audio/visual collaboration between songwriter Line BÃ¸gh and Christian Gundtoft himself.
